  000381                                                                                                                            
  000382                PROCEDURE DIVISION.                                                                                         
  000383                                                                                                                            
  000384               *******************************************************                                                      
  000385               * 0000-MAIN. THIS ROUTINE CONTROLS THE FLOW OF THE    *                                                      
  000386               * PROGRAM. IT CALLS ROUTINES TO SET THE TIME AND DATE,*                                                      
  000387               * READ THE FIRSTS RECORD, SETS THE FUND RECORD, READS *                                                      
  000388               * THE REST OF THE RECORDS IN THE FIRST FILE & WRITES  *                                                      
  000389               * ANY HIGH-SALE BROKERS TO A SEPERATE FILE. AFTER     *                                                      
  000390               * READING ALL OF THE FIRST FILE, THE PROGRAM READS    *                                                      
  000391               * THE HIGH-SALE FILE TO PRINT THE SUMMARY.            *                                                      
  000392               *******************************************************                                                      
  000393                0000-MAIN.                                                                                                  
  000394                                                                                                                            
  000395                    CALL JOBNAME USING JOBNAME.                                           212 212                           
  000396                                                                                                                            
  000397                    PERFORM 0100-DATE-AND-TIME.                                           465                               
  000398                                                                                                                            
  000399                    OPEN INPUT  SALES-FILE                                                49

Context usage is indicated by the letter preceding a procedure-name reference.                                                      
These letters and their meanings are:                                                                                               
    A = ALTER (procedure-name)                                                                                                      
    D = GO TO (procedure-name) DEPENDING ON                                                                                         
    E = End of range of (PERFORM) through (procedure-name)                                                                          
    G = GO TO (procedure-name)                                                                                                      
    P = PERFORM (procedure-name)                                                                                                    
    T = (ALTER) TO PROCEED TO (procedure-name)                                                                                      
    U = USE FOR DEBUGGING (procedure-name)
